          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;

        }

          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;

          box-sizing: border-box;
          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }
        .container-outside {
          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        <h2>Email display settings</h2>

        <p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>

        <p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Tested in Mac chrome with 102.0.4954.0 version.



<span class="line"><!---->Tested in Mac chrome with 102.0.4954.0 version.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





We need to firstly click laboratory icon in the browser, and in Tab Search Media Tabs, select `Enable - Media tabs also shown in Open Tabs Section`. Reboot chrome to enable that feature. (I'm not sure whether that feature is the key to reproduce this UAF)



<span class="line"><!---->We need to firstly click laboratory icon in the browser, and in Tab Search Media Tabs, select `Enable - Media tabs also shown in Open Tabs Section`. Reboot chrome to enable that feature. (I'm not sure whether that feature is the key to reproduce this UAF)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





See video for reproduction. (I'll try to minimize the operation of the reproduction, and will upload the updated one if possible)

From the stack trace and looking at the code, I'm not sure how it got into this state. The use of ScopedMultiSourceObservation should be doing the right thing here. Each observed widget should be sending an OnWidgetClosing() event and that will clean up that specific widget from the SMSO. If another widget is being observed, it will remain in the SMSO and be removed when the SMSO is destroyed.



<span class="line"><!---->From the stack trace and looking at the code, I'm not sure how it got into this state. The use of ScopedMultiSourceObservation should be doing the right thing here. Each observed widget should be sending an OnWidgetClosing() event and that will clean up that specific widget from the SMSO. If another widget is being observed, it will remain in the SMSO and be removed when the SMSO is destroyed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Does this only reproduce on the Mac? I'm unable to repro it on Windows.



<span class="line"><!---->Does this only reproduce on the Mac? I'm unable to repro it on Windows.<!----></span>

kerenzhu@ - what happens if instead of listening to OnWidgetClosing(), listen to OnWidgetDestroying()? OnWidgetClosing() may not be called if Widget::CloseNow() or Widget::Close() aren't called. This can happen if the NativeWidget initiates the closure. OnWidgetDestroying() is called right before the Widget is destroyed.



<span class="line"><!---->kerenzhu@ - what happens if instead of listening to OnWidgetClosing(), listen to OnWidgetDestroying()? OnWidgetClosing() may not be called if Widget::CloseNow() or Widget::Close() aren't called. This can happen if the NativeWidget initiates the closure. OnWidgetDestroying() is called right before the Widget is destroyed.<!----></span>

wow, I think you've found the right fix. Indeed, OnWidgetClosing() is not called for closure initiated by the OS, so MediaRouterDialogControllerViews won't stop observing the widget after it's been destroyed. 



<span class="line"><!---->wow, I think you've found the right fix. Indeed, OnWidgetClosing() is not called for closure initiated by the OS, so MediaRouterDialogControllerViews won't stop observing the widget after it's been destroyed. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I think the more fundamental problem is that ScopedMultiSourceObservation does not provide safe guarantee when observer outlives observee. This is the same root cause of UaF found in ComboboxModel, 



<span class="line"><!---->I think the more fundamental problem is that ScopedMultiSourceObservation does not provide safe guarantee when observer outlives observee. This is the same root cause of UaF found in ComboboxModel, <!----></span>





crbug.com/1264288



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1264288" title="views::Combobox(ui::ComboboxModel*) is prone to UAF"><!---->crbug.com/1264288<!----></a>

Removing review request labels. I think this issue has little security impact and therefore the patch is not qualified for a branch merge. 



<span class="line"><!---->Removing review request labels. I think this issue has little security impact and therefore the patch is not qualified for a branch merge. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Specifically, we were not able to reproduce the crash. The patch was made as a best-effort guesswork, by identifying and fixing the cause from the stacktrace provided by happyercat@. The patch includes a test where the crashing state is simulated, but I believe it never happens in reality.



<span class="line"><!---->Specifically, we were not able to reproduce the crash. The patch was made as a best-effort guesswork, by identifying and fixing the cause from the stacktrace provided by happyercat@. The patch includes a test where the crashing state is simulated, but I believe it never happens in reality.<!----></span>

Hi team, I think it is still a High Severity issue based on the following points:



<span class="line"><!---->Hi team, I think it is still a High Severity issue based on the following points:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Since 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Since <!----></span>





issue 1249491



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1249491" title="use after free in ash::sharesheet::SharesheetBubbleView::CloseBubble"><!---->issue 1249491<!----></a>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>





uses similar user interaction and rated as High Severity, I wonder whether the "the user interaction required" affect its Security_Severity to low. All the user interaction here is trigger Cast dialog twice. (I'm not sure if there exists an API for extension to open Cast Dialog or request Cast, if it exists, it doesn't needs user interaction anymore.) The moving/closing tab user interaction could be done by extension as described in the next point.



<span class="line"><!---->uses similar user interaction and rated as High Severity, I wonder whether the "the user interaction required" affect its Security_Severity to low. All the user interaction here is trigger Cast dialog twice. (I'm not sure if there exists an API for extension to open Cast Dialog or request Cast, if it exists, it doesn't needs user interaction anymore.) The moving/closing tab user interaction could be done by extension as described in the next point.<!----></span>



<br>





2. I think it is remote exploitable, since the extension could move one tab to another window and close that tab page, in order to trigger the UAF. 



<span class="line"><!---->2. I think it is remote exploitable, since the extension could move one tab to another window and close that tab page, in order to trigger the UAF. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Please let me know if I was incorrect. Many thanks.



<span class="line"><!---->Please let me know if I was incorrect. Many thanks.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

<span class="line"><!---->Hi team, I've updated the PoC. All the user-interaction needed here is to open the Cast dialog. To reproduce:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Install the attached extension.



<span class="line"><!---->1. Install the attached extension.<!----></span>



<br>





2. When the new page opened, open Cast dialog.



<span class="line"><!---->2. When the new page opened, open Cast dialog.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Wait for several seconds, the UAF happens.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Wait for several seconds, the UAF happens.<!----></span>

Hi there, I've made another simplified PoC which only need to click the button once in the page and is more convincing in terms of the user-interaction. To reproduce the new PoC:



<span class="line"><!---->Hi there, I've made another simplified PoC which only need to click the button once in the page and is more convincing in terms of the user-interaction. To reproduce the new PoC:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Install the attached extension and host the poc.html (or you could change the url to {url:'poc.html'} in media.js to omit the host step).



<span class="line"><!---->1. Install the attached extension and host the poc.html (or you could change the url to {url:'poc.html'} in media.js to omit the host step).<!----></span>



<br>





2. When the new page opened, click the "Trigger" button.



<span class="line"><!---->2. When the new page opened, click the "Trigger" button.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Wait for several seconds, the UAF happens.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Wait for several seconds, the UAF happens.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Tested on 102.0.4954.0 version as well. I've attached a video to demonstrate the reproduction. All user interaction needed here is only **click the "Trigger" button once**. 



<span class="line"><!---->Tested on 102.0.4954.0 version as well. I've attached a video to demonstrate the reproduction. All user interaction needed here is only **click the "Trigger" button once**. <!----></span>



<br>





Moreover, since the PoC leverage the PresentationRequest to trigger the dialog, the UAF trace stack is slightly different than the original one. Thank you.



<span class="line"><!---->Moreover, since the PoC leverage the PresentationRequest to trigger the dialog, the UAF trace stack is slightly different than the original one. Thank you.<!----></span>
